Recent Situation in the Min-Gan-Yue Border Area Bandit Suppression 73

Shantou Dispatch: The communist bandits' invasion of northern Guangdong has failed, and their main force has retreated to their old nests in Huichang, Ruijin, and Yudu. The bandit suppression army of Guangdong Province is determined to cooperate effectively with the central government and the Hunan-Jiangxi armies, dividing into two columns, preparing to directly encircle and suppress the bandits. In the future, the main battle will undoubtedly trend towards the intersection of the three provinces of Fujian, Jiangxi, and Guangdong. Currently, the Jiangxi bandits are also active in western Fujian. The Red bandit's 12th Army under Luo Binghui's command in Changting, on July 15th, invaded Yongding Kanshi and Longtan. The local militia fought against the bandits based on their fortifications. However, due to being outnumbered, they were defeated by the bandits. The local militia in Xiayang Zhongkeng and other places, seeing the ferocity of the bandits, did not dare to resist and fled into the mountains. Luo's bandits then advanced straight into Zhongkeng, the hometown of Hu Wenhu of Yong An Tang. The local militia there numbered about 1,000, with sufficient guns and cannons, but they also did not dare to resist the bandits and retreated to the border area of Sixian and Datian County Hutousha in Guangdong. The bandits destroyed the militia fortifications, burned civilian houses, and kidnapped about 2,000 to 3,000 refugees, imprisoning them in Chen Dong Township. Since the 20th, Fujian refugees have fled into Datian County in Guangdong Province. The county magistrate, Liang Ruogu, seeing this situation, telegraphed Huang Yanzhen, commander of the 7th Division of Meixian, for help, as the county had only two battalions of troops stationed there, and their forces were weak. Huang immediately dispatched Luo Zhichun of the Training Corps on the 25th to Datian to defend the area. Because of this, rumors inevitably arose. Furthermore, the regiment of Zhong Junfang, commander of the 2nd Independent Division stationed in the city, besieged the bandits in Huangtian, Xunwu, on the 18th. The Red bandits there, consisting of the 8th Regiment and the Red Guards, numbering 600 to 700, retreated towards Huangxiang on the 21st, disturbing our Xuxi, and engaged Zhong's regiment until noon. The bandits were defeated and fled towards the Hejiao area. The above is the situation on the Guangdong-Jiangxi border. Secondly, several hundred Red bandits under Gu Dacun's command are lurking in the mountains of Jiulongzhang, Houdong, Yangxikeng, etc., making counter-revolutionary propaganda speeches everywhere and oppressing the villagers to join the Red ranks. This is truly a disaster for the heartland of Chaozhou and Meizhou. The various armies are currently planning to advance and suppress them, and the local police forces of each county have also re-established joint defense and stepped up their work. The bandit suppression situation currently seems to be gradually improving. Once the central government armies are completely concentrated and the 19th Route Army arrives in western Fujian, the Red bandits will have no ability to invade.

Welcome to the 19th Route Army by All Sectors in Shizhong 74

The Red Bandits Fled at the News

Shizhong Dispatch: All of the 5th Regiment of the 120th Brigade of the 60th Division of the 19th Route Army arrived in Heshi yesterday, the 25th, from Longshan, and arrived in Shizhong this morning. Those who went to Lezhi Pavilion to welcome them included the deputy leader of the security team, Lin Xiantang, the deputy leader Xie Yangqiu, and representatives from various agencies and groups, Shizhong Public School, the Boy Scout

Page 11

Corps, Long　Public School, Dunzhu Public School,　　　Public School, etc. More than 1,000 students from various schools. At around 10 o'clock, the Commander Zuo Xun personally led all the officers and soldiers of the regiment to arrive, and the discipline was very strict. Commander Liang, dressed in a gray military uniform, was very sincere in his attitude and shook hands with each of the welcoming representatives as a courtesy. He frequently smiled and nodded to the welcoming people and young students and said, "You should treat me as a Shizhong person, not as an outsider, and don't be polite. We need to realize cooperation between the military and the people," etc. Slogans of welcome were posted everywhere, colorful and eye-catching. All agencies, schools, and civilian houses and shops along the way flew flags and banners to show their welcome. When Commander Liang and the welcoming representatives from all walks of life walked along Sucheng Road and Baoan Road to the security team's office, firecrackers exploded and cheers rang out, showing the enthusiasm of the people at that time. The regimental headquarters is located at the Dazhong Academy on Sucheng Road. Commander Liang, Deputy Commander Zhong, and Deputy Commander Tan rested briefly at the security team's office, and then Deputy Commander Lin Xiantang accompanied them to the regimental headquarters. Commander Liang inquired in detail about the bandit situation in the vicinity. The regiment has more than 2,500 people in total. After arriving in Shizhong, they went to various mountain passes to deploy defenses to replace the security team, allowing them to rest temporarily. The Red bandits in the Longtan Tiandi area, upon hearing that the 19th Route Army had arrived in Shizhong, retreated to Changliu Kanshi, leaving only a few local Red bandits in that area. The bandits in Shanpingtou also retreated to Hexi, and the bandits in Juzhou also retreated to Lantangkang. The Red bandits in Iwaki City have not dared to stay in the city for long in recent nights. Currently, the areas of Hexi, Wangzhuang, and Zhanglai are heavily guarded, but the situation is very panic-stricken. (July 26)

Local Correspondence

Songjiang 75

Breaking a Local Opium Smuggling Case and Escorting Suspects to Songjiang: Tinglin Town in Punan County is a prosperous commercial center, but it is rife with gambling and opium, and there are also harmful drugs in circulation, which are a scourge to society. Huang Xinyi, chief of the First Public Security Branch in the area, recently received reports that Liu Qiugen, the owner of a certain pharmacy, was engaged in opium smuggling and was making a thriving living. He sent police officers to search the premises, and they found two large pieces of opium weighing more than 40 taels in the shop. Liu Qiugen was arrested and escorted to the county Public Security Bureau for preliminary interrogation, and then transferred to the county court for questioning. It is reported that the prosecutor's office pre-trialed the case, and the defendant denied smuggling opium, claiming that it was deposited by others, etc. He is currently detained in the detention center for verification.

Taicang 76

Theater Performance to Raise Funds Leads to Brawls Among Spectators: Recently, bandits have risen in this county. The people of the four villages, in order to seek self-defense, are expanding the original security regiment to supplement the insufficiency of the police force, but they are suffering from a lack of funds. Subsequently, after public discussion among the local people, a Zhejiang opera troupe was invited to Taicang to perform, and the surplus funds would be used to recruit members and purchase firearms for the security regiment. July 31st was the sixth day of the performance in Shatou Town. Just as the performance was about to begin, some people intended to enter the theater without purchasing tickets. The organizers advised them to desist, but to no avail. They swarmed into the theater, causing public anger and leading to conflicts. More than ten spectators, including Wang Bingkun, were beaten and injured, and order was immediately disrupted. Fortunately, the Hewei Regiment made great efforts to mediate, and the storm was finally calmed.

Kunshan 77

New Director of Finance Bureau Takes Office: Since Li Fajhen resigned as the Director of the Finance Bureau of this county, County Magistrate Cheng Ruji has been concurrently holding the position. Now, the provincial government has appointed Hu Baoxing to take over. After being appointed, Hu sent a telegram to pay his respects to County Magistrate Cheng on the 1st and then took office.

Election of County Executive and Supervisory Committee Members: After the opening of the Fifth Kunshan County

Representative Congress on the 30th, the election of the Executive and Supervisory Committee members for this term was originally scheduled for the morning of the 1st. However, due to various reasons, the election could not be held within the prescribed time, and the meeting was postponed twice. The election finally took place at 4:30 p.m. As a result, Gu Yugui, Zhang Jianqian, and Cai Wuzai were elected as Executive Committee members, Wang Dasan and Ma Bingtain were elected as Alternate Executive Committee members, Sheng Minghe was elected as Supervisory Committee member, and Li Ziyi was elected as Alternate Supervisory Committee member.

Nantong 78

Governance and Transport Loan Established: The provincial government ordered the county to borrow and allocate 52,500 yuan for the governance and transport water fund. In addition to transferring the funds raised from the road construction mu tax, the county government established a six-month short-term loan of 10,000 yuan from various banks in Nantong on the 1st, with a monthly interest rate of 8%, using the provincial government's busy Cao mortgage bonds as collateral, and transferred them to the provincial government for reserve.

Problem of Demolishing the Tonghai Telephone Line: The commercial long-distance telephone line between Nantong and Haimen was ordered to be demolished by the ministry because the regulations were not in compliance. Currently, merchants and residents of the two counties have submitted a request to the county, asking it to forward it to the province and consult the ministry to allow the line to be spared demolition.

Wuxi 79

New Education Bureau Chief Takes Office: The newly appointed Education Bureau Chief of this county, Zang Hu (Buddhist Roots), arrived in Wuxi on the 30th of last month. Yesterday (the 1st), at 8:00 AM, Chief Zang, accompanied by receiving specialists Hua Jinji, Xin Bolin, and Zang Jia San, went directly to the Education Bureau located in Zongqiao. They were greeted by the former Chief Lu, who led them to the reception room for a brief discussion of transfer procedures and the current state of education. Then, they proceeded upstairs to the Bureau Chief's office, where the official seal, files, money, supplies, documents, books, etc., were handed over one by one. Chief Zang received them. This process lasted for two hours before it was completed. After the reception, Chief Zang will submit a report to the County Government, which will forward it to the Education Department for record.

Report of Merchants Trafficking in Enemy Goods: The County Chamber of Commerce of this county received a letter from Zhang Yifen, Lu Jiangui, Chen Tianmin, Jiang Shihen, Huang Fangzhou, and others stating that the three merchants of Beitaing, Xie Dasen, Qinyu, and Yunhua, as well as the unscrupulous merchants like Shen Jinyan of Si Bao Qiao Da Wang Miao, have been continuously transporting large quantities of enemy goods to Wuxi, with transactions amounting to tens of thousands of yuan each. The transportation methods include trains, steamships, and rice and wheat boats, with the latter being the most common. Moreover, certain factories raise the prices of domestic goods whenever there is a boycott of Japanese goods, even making a profit of more than ten yuan per bolt. Swiss national government silk sells for 41 cents per yard, while certain factory government silk sells for 61 cents per yard. The former is four cents one fen, far surpassing 61 cents. This is just one example. All other factories are also taking this opportunity to raise prices. Just like this, towards the country... naturally... The reason why enemy goods... cannot... merchants... worthy of... Xie factories also cannot escape blame. The intention is to strictly ban the cotton trafficking in enemy goods, and to suppress the price of domestic goods, etc. After receiving the letter, the Chamber of Commerce yesterday forwarded it to the silk and cloth industry association, for quick notification, so as to be easy to report.

Changzhou 80

A Step-Mother Murders Her Son in the Sixth District: Qian Jingda of Datangli Village, Maoyan Township, Sixth District, Wu County, married Lu, who was driven out to work as a helper by Jingda's stepmother. Recently, on the 25th of last month, Lu found her husband...seven orifices bleeding, the entire body in bruises, asking for justice. After waking from the shock, she returned home to inquire. It was confirmed that her husband had indeed been murdered by his stepmother, Wang, and his uncle, Qian Genlin, along with their sons, Longxu and Xukun. There was also a close relative, Hu Yongqin, as a witness. Lu, grieving for her husband, immediately reported it to the nearby police station. Qian Wangshi and Qian Genlin were arrested, and on the 1st, they were taken to the County Court for interrogation. The supervising prosecutor led officials to the village today (the 2nd) to open the coffin for a post-mortem examination to verify the facts.

Zhenjiang 81

Implementing the Dredging Plan: In recent years, due to geographical changes and upstream erosion in the Yangtze River channel, the downstream areas, such as Zhenjiang and Jiangyin, have seen increasing accumulation of sandbars in the river's center, hindering navigation. The central government established a Yangtze River Waterway Management Committee, but due to financial constraints, construction has been delayed. In Zhenjiang, for example, sandbars are scattered everywhere in the river's center, and many areas along the riverbank are also silted up, preventing small steamers and boats from docking. This is a major obstacle to transportation. Zhenjiang has formed a River Dredging Committee, organized by the Chamber of Commerce, Shipping Association, Water Conservancy Bureau (now joined by the Construction Department), and Construction Bureau, to plan the dredging of the river channel. The funding for implementation comes from surcharges on small steamer passenger tickets. It is reported that more than 70,000 yuan has been collected to date (but half should be allocated for the use of administration). The committee also recognizes that the silting of the river beaches is becoming increasingly serious and should be dredged as soon as possible. It has already purchased a dredger and is engaged in dredging. It is estimated that the entire project along the river will take about three months to complete.

Hangzhou 82

Measures for Punishing Concealment of Land Taxes: The Zhejiang Provincial Government considers land tax revenue to be an important part of the province's income. The annual regular tax, surcharges, and special donations amount to approximately 9 million yuan. Although the province's land has not been fully surveyed, it is estimated that the total amount of land tax concealed, evaded, and in arrears is approximately 20 million yuan. To improve revenue and replenish the provincial treasury, a research group was organized, and a committee for recovering old debts was established to vigorously rectify the situation. The following measures for punishing people in Zhejiang Province who conceal land and evade land taxes were specifically formulated: (1) Except as otherwise provided by law, the punishment for the concealment of cultivated land taxes by individuals or groups shall be handled in accordance with these measures. (2) If any of the following circumstances exist and the relevant government agency issues a public notice but the land tax is still not paid or the transfer of ownership is not reported after the deadline, the land shall be confiscated: 1. Those who have defaulted on land tax for years and refuse to pay; 2. Those who inherit land but do not complete the transfer of ownership and pay land tax in accordance with the regulations or have no land deed; 3. Those who own land with or without land tax but conceal it and do not report it. (3) Land confiscated by a government agency in accordance with the preceding article shall be evaluated and sold by the competent tax authority. After deducting the amount of land tax owed over the years from the land price, the remaining amount shall be allocated to local education and autonomy projects. The distribution method will be determined separately. (4) If a land without land tax is discovered as a result of a report, 20% of the value of the confiscated land may be given to the informant. If it is reported by a tenant farmer or farmer and confirmed, the original informant may be granted the right to manage and pay the land tax without compensation. (5) If a person voluntarily reports land with or without land tax to the competent tax authority and it is verified that there is no fraud or other entanglement, he or she shall be allowed to pay the land tax from the date of the voluntary report at the ratio of the nearby farmland tax rate, and the past shall be exempted from prosecution.

Shaoxing 83

Bandits from Sheng County Burn and Loot Wangxiewan: Wangxiewan, located in the fourth district of Shaoxing and bordering Sheng County, was suddenly attacked by more than a dozen bandits from Sheng County a month ago. They attempted to kidnap Zheng Jinshun's young son, but Zheng was alerted and escaped through the back door. The bandits suspected that he had fled to Zheng Hailin's house next door. Because the doors were tightly closed, they could not enter, so they set the house on fire to vent their anger. The area mainly consisted of thatched huts, and once a fire started, it could not be contained. It spread to more than 30 households. The Director of the Public Security Bureau arrived at the scene of the incident on the 31st to investigate and ordered the village chief to report the affected households for relief purposes.

Xiaoshan 84

A Boat Robbed at Sanjiangkou: On the night of the 29th, a boat sailing from Zhuji to Xiaoshan, fully loaded with groceries, rice, wheat, and four passengers, was en route to Yiqiao. Suddenly, it was met by a pirate ship coming head-on. As soon as it reached the boat, six bandits armed with quick-firing guns jumped aboard and looted everything. Five foreign letters, 120 yuan in foreign currency, six catties of white silk, and more than ten catties of tea were taken away. The bandits also searched the passengers, taking more than 70 yuan in large and small silver coins and a gold ring. As dawn approached, they fired a warning shot, disembarked, and fled north.

Husband and Wife Quarrel, Both Die: In Yantou near Qianqing in the eastern township of Xiaoshan, a farmer, Zhu Zuqi, asked his wife, Wang, to hire workers from her mother's family because the weather was hot and the fields were dry. Unexpectedly, when Wang returned from her mother's family on the 30th, no one could be hired. As a result, the couple began to quarrel. During the night, Zuqi, in anger, beat his wife. Unexpectedly, the blow hit a vital point, and she died on the spot. On the morning of the 31st, her husband regretted what he had done and drowned himself in the pond in the backyard. He left behind one son and two daughters, all of whom were young. Their cries for their mother and father were heartbreaking.

Bengbu 85

Anhui Province is experiencing a Severe Plague: The weather has been scorching hot in recent months, and a severe plague is spreading in northern Anhui, with successive deaths. The situation is worsening. Since its discovery in Bengbu last month, an estimated 300 people have been infected, mostly poor people and laborers. Patients who are not taken to the hospital for treatment within two hours cannot be saved. Recently, it has spread to the Huai River basin, including Huaiyuan, Luohe, Fengzhi, and Wuhe, with great ferocity. The Flood Relief Committee's epidemic prevention team of the National Government has dispatched personnel to these areas to carry out epidemic prevention and vaccination work.

Hefei 86

The Town of Sanhe Breaks Through Two Weirs: The polder fields along the inner river of Chaohu in Hefei were at risk of flooding in the first half of the month. Recently, the situation has gradually stabilized. However, the weirs of Sanhe Town, Yongxing, Yonggu, Fengzhou, Fengzhi, and Fengtai on the south bank of Hunan are still at great risk due to their low-lying terrain. Xu Shu, the chief of the county's disaster relief, urgently took 3,000 yuan to supervise the workers in strengthening the embankments for rescue. However, due to the large waves, the Yongxing and Yonggu weirs were tragically breached the night before. Dozens of miles of ripe crops were washed away. Xu is now sending people to transport 4,000 yuan from the city to rescue the Zhaofu, Fengzhi, and other weirs that have not yet been breached.

Education News

Important News

A Record of the Second Day of the Chemistry Discussion Meeting 87

The Minimum Standard for Junior High School Chemistry Curriculum Determined. Universities to Add Lectureships in National Defense Chemistry Research. Nanjing, 2nd Dispatch: The Ministry of Education's Chemistry Discussion Meeting continued in a general assembly this morning, chaired by Chen Kezhong. Li Yunhua from Qinghua University, Chen Fugang from Jinling University, Huang Xinyan from the University of Hong Kong, Lin Dazhong from Kai Cheng Company, and Wang Jiliang from the Central Research Institute successively reported on the chemical equipment and work in various places. At 10:30 AM, the Proposal Consolidation Committee convened, and in the afternoon, group meetings were held. The Curriculum Standards Group, chaired by Zeng Zhaolun, discussed and determined the minimum standard for the junior high school chemistry curriculum and the main goals and points to note for the senior high school curriculum. The National Defense Chemistry Group, chaired by Huang Xinyan, passed three important proposals: (1) This conference should request the Ministry of Education to select and prepare at least four complete universities to add lectureships in national defense chemistry research and assistantships for research on military poisonous gas, smoke screens, and the defense of incendiary gas. (2) Request the Ministry of Education to submit an order to the government instructing universities and other academic research institutions to independently establish national defense chemistry lectureships and research laboratories within their capabilities. (3) Request the government to establish a national defense chemistry institution under the Ministry of Military Affairs.

Chen Shizhen Temporarily Concurrently Serves as Director of Higher Education Department 88

Guo Xin Song's Leave is Over and Has No Intention of Returning Nanjing, 2nd Dispatch: Guo Xin Song, Director of the Higher Education Department of the Ministry of Education, has overstayed his leave and has no intention of returning. On the 2nd, the Ministry of Education ordered Chen Shizhen, a counselor, to temporarily concurrently serve as the Director of the Higher Education Department, and also ordered Lu Hanqin, an inspector, to temporarily concurrently serve as the Chief of the Second Section of the Higher Education Department.

A Record of the Second Day of the Elementary and Secondary School Curriculum Standards Meeting 89

The Credit System is Abolished in Junior and Senior High Schools, and Class Hours are Used for Calculation. Time for Each Subject is Re-Allocated. Party Principles is Changed to Civics. Elementary Schools Add Civic Training Courses, with All Teachers Responsible Nanjing, 2nd Dispatch: The Curriculum Standards Revision Committee for Elementary and Secondary Schools held meetings at the Ministry of Education both in the morning and afternoon of the 2nd. The attending members were the same as before.

(1) Middle School Group: The Middle School Group, chaired by Gu Shusen, resolved in the morning:

(A) The credit system in junior and senior high schools is abolished, and class hours are used for calculation; (B) The class hours for each subject in junior high school are re-allocated as follows: 1. Each semester generally has 36 hours of instruction per week; 2. Party Principles is changed to Civics, with the same number of class hours; 3. Chinese language is generally taught for six hours per week in each semester; 4. Mathematics is generally taught with mixed textbooks and can also adopt a mixed system or a subject-based system. Physics and chemistry are listed separately, and each is taught in one school year, with four hours of instruction per week in each semester. 6. Physiology and hygiene are changed to health, with one hour of instruction per week in each semester; 7. Geography is generally taught for two hours per week in each semester; 8. The other subjects remain the same.

(C) The format of the middle school curriculum standards is stipulated as follows: 1. Standards are divided into three parts: objectives, teaching material outline, and time allocation; 2. The implementation methods are generally divided into work requirements, teaching method points, and the minimum graduation requirements. The details of each subject should not be too far apart. In the afternoon, a meeting was held to discuss the senior high school subject time allocation table. The opinions of each person were roughly divided into three categories: 1. Senior high school should only have one type of general compulsory subject, except for vocational and normal schools; 2. To adapt to individuality and habits, subjects should be divided into liberal arts and science from the first year of senior high school, each with compulsory and elective subjects; 3. The first and second years are not divided into subjects, and the division into liberal arts and science starts in the third year. Experts and educators from various departments and subjects among the committee members each have their own subjective and firm opinions. The debate over whether or not to divide into subjects was quite heated. The discussion continued until after 5:00 PM without any results. Finally, it was decided to recommend Dai Yingguan and Li Yiyan to redraft the senior high school subject time allocation table. Another meeting will be held at 8:00 AM on the 3rd to discuss it.

Health Experts Express Dissatisfaction 90

Thirty-Six Hours of Instruction per Week Will Be Reconsidered Today

According to health educators, the decision made today to have 36 hours of instruction per week, with experts from each subject fighting for more hours for their own subjects, will ultimately sacrifice the health of young people across the country and have a huge impact on the survival of the nation. It was decided on the 3rd to jointly propose a reconsideration of the case of the junior high school instruction hours in the hope of reducing the instruction time.

(2) Elementary School Group

The Elementary School Group, chaired by Wu Yanin, resolved in the morning: (A) Continue to discuss and revise the curriculum standards outline; (B) Add a civic training course, placing it before health (the first meeting decided to add a moral education standards proposal, renamed the civic training course standards, still drafted by Xue Tianhan, etc.) The main points are as follows: 1. The purpose is to train character and behavior; 2. Two guidance sessions are scheduled each week (guidance on etiquette, practice, and behavior); 3. Civic training opportunities should be provided at any time in group activities (such as class meetings and morning meetings); 4. In addition to the homeroom teacher being specifically responsible for training, all teachers in the school must be responsible for guidance; 5. The key points of the training method should state that textbooks are not allowed, and only teaching methods for teachers should be compiled; 6. Civic training should be based on specific standards, using pictures, stories, music, etc. to guide children and implement it effectively.

(C) Compile the outline of the civic training course as follows: 1. Objectives 2. Specific standards, divided into three stages: low, medium, and high, summarized into several items; 3. Key points of the training method;

(D) Determine the meeting schedule: discuss in the morning and review in the afternoon of the 3rd, discuss the civic training curriculum standards on the 4th, hold a general discussion on the 5th, and hold a general assembly on the 6th. Sub-committee review meetings will be held in the afternoon of the 2nd, and the meetings will adjourn at 5:00 PM.

American Black Man Tolan Sets New 100m Record 93

Time of 10.3 Seconds Sets a New Games Record

And Equals the World Record

(Electric Communications News Agency, Los Angeles, 1st Dispatch) The results of today's 100m final are: 1st: Tolan (USA) 10.3 seconds (New Olympic Record)

2nd: Metcalfe (USA) 3rd: Jonath (Germany) 4th: Simpson (USA) 5th: Toerien (South Africa) 6th: Yoshioka Ryuto (Japan) 10.6 seconds (Electric Communications News Agency, Los Angeles, 1st Dispatch) In today's schedule, the 100m final, which attracted the most attention, was, as generally expected, won by the American black athlete Tolan (also translated as Turen). The American flag was raised again on the central flagpole. His results are as follows:

1st: Tolan (USA) 10.3 seconds (Olympic Record) 2nd: Metcalfe (USA) 3rd: Jonath (Germany)

The Competition Process: The course of this fierce battle is roughly as follows: The American starter made two corrections to the start, and the race did not start until the third time. Japan's Yoshioka had an excellent start and led the way in the first 40 meters. At 50 meters, they were neck and neck, forming a single group. At 70 meters, Yoshioka fell to fourth place, and his final sprint did not go as planned. He finished sixth, one meter behind fifth place. According to external criticism, he sprinted too hard in the first half, making it difficult to continue later. Yoshioka, who finished sixth and earned one point, told reporters, "Both the semi-final and the final were difficult. I am very disappointed with the track. The starting method should be ideal, but at 70 meters, I was overtaken by those behind me. Perhaps it was due to the difference in physical strength, and I could not recover. I am very disappointed."

Electric Communications News Agency, Los Angeles, 1st Dispatch: Today's 100m final was the most exciting for the audience, and the competition was extremely fierce. Tolan (USA) and Metcalfe (USA), two black athletes, are both world record holders with 10.2 seconds, so the competition was very intense. At 50 meters, the two passed Yoshioka (Japan), Jonath (Germany), Simpson (USA), 球佩尔脱 (South Africa), and other athletes. Finally, Tolan won, only two inches ahead of second-place Metcalfe.

Equals World Record: Los Angeles, 1st - Special Dispatch: The 100m final was held at 3:00 PM. The center of attention for this final was to see to what extent the Japanese athlete Yoshioka could compete with Tolan and Metcalfe. After the gun fired, Yoshioka sprinted extremely well and maintained this momentum until 30 meters. However, from the 50-meter mark, his physical strength gradually declined, and he fell to last place at 90 meters. In the end, Tolan (USA) won first place with a time of 10.3 seconds, equaling the world record.

Results of the 100m Semi-Final: Los Angeles, 1st - Special Dispatch: The final preliminary round of the 100m was held today. After the start, Japanese athlete Yoshioka charged forward fiercely, followed by American star Tolan. Yoshioka and Tolan were one meter apart. Everyone expected Yoshioka to take first place. However, at the 70-meter mark, Tolan made an amazing effort and caught up with Yoshioka.

Wrestling Results 99

(Telecommunications, Los Angeles, 1st) The wrestling (freestyle) competition, delayed from the scheduled time, began at 6:10 PM in the indoor gymnasium. Japan's Taniya and Canada's Stock were in the same group. Taniya initially took the offensive, causing Stock to fall. Taniya then jumped in, engaging in a mutual embrace before Stock stood up. Taniya then forcefully threw Stock over his back. National Sports Conference 107

- The Sixth Preparatory Committee Meeting was Held Yesterday -

Drafting of National Sports Implementation Plan: Wu Yunrui Arrives in Beijing to Review Proposals Nanjing, 2nd. At 4 PM on the 2nd, the National Sports Association held its sixth preparatory committee meeting. Preparatory Committee member Wu Yunrui arrived in Beijing with a large volume of the drafted National Sports Implementation Plan, tens of thousands of words in length. He attended the meeting and reported on the process of drafting the plan in Beijing. Chu Minyi, the chairman, reported that 35 proposals had been received from all parties, totaling 98 items. The Ministry of Education was consulted to respond to the members' request for half-price ship tickets. The China Merchants Bureau has been ordered to comply. The Standard Sports Equipment Company replied that more than 200 pieces of domestic sports equipment are packed in five large boxes and will be transported to Beijing for display before the conference. The following resolutions were made: (1) Regarding the association's funding, please request the Ministry of Education to telegraph Song Ziwen, the Minister of Finance, to allocate funds quickly. (2) The Chinese Sports Association and the Shanghai Jingwu Sports Association are permitted to attend as special attendees. (3) Each secondary school and above in Tianjin is permitted to send one representative to Beijing to attend. (4) Technical colleges that have not been registered are not permitted to attend. (5) During the conference, special attention should be paid to the National Sports Law. (6) A temporary proposal consolidation committee will be organized by the preparatory committee and several experts and members hired separately, with Wu Yunrui responsible for convening. (7) Members arriving in Beijing before August 15 should report to the Ministry of Education. Those arriving after the 16th should report to the Lizhi Society.

Yesterday, the Educational Community of this City Gave a Farewell to the Educational Inspection Group Going to Europe 109

The Ministry of Education, in response to a request from the League of Nations, has specially sent Cheng Qibao, Chen Hexian, Yang Lian, Li Ximou, Li Jiaxiang, Guo Youshou, Cao Kang, and others to Europe to investigate education. It has been decided that they will set off on the 5th of this month. The educational community of this city held a farewell party at the Tsinghua Alumni Association at 5 PM yesterday to discuss educational issues. Xu Peihuang, Liu Zhanen, Ou Yuanhuai, Zhu Shaoping, Dong Renjian, Pan Guangdan, Li Zhaohuan, Quan Zengha, and others attended, totaling several dozen people. Ou Yuanhuai chaired the meeting and delivered a farewell speech, saying that today, we are seeing off Cheng Qibao and others to Europe to investigate education. We deeply understand that Mr. Cheng and others have rich knowledge, and this trip will definitely achieve good results and contribute to the educational world of our country. Next, Liu Zhanen, Xu Peihuang, Li Zhaohuan, Pan Guangdan, Shen Xinqing, Huang Jingen, Xie Xunchu, and others also gave earnest speeches, requesting that Mr. Cheng and others focus on the characteristics of foreign education during this trip to Europe, especially on civic education. Then, Mr. Cheng and others gave reply speeches.

Gold Price Drops: Four Taels and Three Mace 110

Fluctuations of Six Taels Throughout the City: Gold price continued its decline in yesterday's trading, with a fluctuation of six taels, but no major movements. By day's end, it fell by four taels. The sentiment among traders was weak, with supply exceeding demand. Initially, the silver market rose against the British pound and the US dollar, causing exchange rates to increase. The market opened lower but experienced temporary advances and retreats. The foreign exchange market remained unchanged on the surface, but internally it loosened. Particularly, the widespread selling by major players caused prices to decline further. It eventually dropped to the 740-tael mark. The market then rose slightly by a little over two taels due to purchases by Guangdong merchants. However, exchange rates stabilized. Rumors circulated that a certain bank had received 4,900 cash bars. Yu Fengyong and others had previously sold these bars, and yesterday, as usual, they released about 5,800 public certificates (i.e., spot gold), including over 2,500 taels by Dade Cheng, 400-500 taels each by Qian Changxiang and Dafeng Heng, over 800 taels by Tong Feng Heng, and over 500 taels by Ruixing. As for those who received the bars, Zhifeng Yong received about 2,000, Run Changyu received 1,400-1,500, Yifeng Yong received over 400, and Yuan Xingyong received over 900. Therefore, the spot gold market seemed to be well-supplied. However, the forward premium only increased by 8 taels, and some traders made transactions. Massive Selling Wave Discovered in Cotton Market 116

Impact of US Cotton Inventory Announcement

The cotton market plummeted, with the downward trend intensifying. This was triggered by the announcement of US cotton inventories, which amounted to 13,449,000 bales, an increase of over 4 million bales compared to last year. This news greatly shocked the local market, leading to expectations of a price decline in US cotton. Speculators rushed to sell short, causing panic in the market. However, the price of US cotton remained stable, and some major players aggressively bought long positions. However, the majority of market participants believed that US cotton inventories were too high, limiting the potential for price increases, and therefore leaned towards expecting a decline. The future direction of the market will continue to depend on the movements of US cotton.

Zheng Brand Falls by 7 Qian: In the pre-market trading of Zheng Brand cotton, the market atmosphere was good due to stable US cotton prices. However, in the second and third rounds of trading, the news of US cotton inventories arrived, causing widespread panic and a sharp decline in the market. As a result, the prices for all months fell by 5.5 to 7 qian. The total trading volume was 58,300 dan. Overview of Hubei Cotton Production 119

Cotton Fields Reduced by Approximately 20-30% Compared to Last Year According to a report released by a Japanese trading company, there was excessive rainfall and low temperatures in various cotton-producing areas during the planting season in mid-May. Frequent rain followed planting. Recently, the climate has recovered, raising hopes for a normal crop. Cotton fields have been reduced by 20-30% compared to last year due to the poor cotton harvests of the past three years, the decline in foreign cotton prices, and the widespread banditry, which hinders farming. The situation in various regions is as follows: Han River Basin: Reduced by 30% compared to last year. Hometown: Reduced by 20%. Zaoyang Suizhou: No change. Pinghan Railway Line: Reduced by 20%. Shashi: No significant difference. Yangtze River Basin: Reduced by 40%.

Italy May Return Boxer Indemnity 129

New Envoy to Present Credentials Date Yet to Be Determined

Since the September 18th Incident, the financial situation of the National Government has been strained. Customs revenues from the three northeastern provinces have been successively seized, further depleting the national treasury. Therefore, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs contacted the United Kingdom, the United States, and Italy to request a one-year deferral of the Boxer Indemnity payments from March of this year to February of next year. All three countries have agreed. A Central News Agency reporter met with personnel from the Italian Embassy's Shanghai office yesterday. According to them, Sino-Italian relations have always been harmonious. Regarding the Boxer Indemnity issue, when Shen Ruilin was the Minister of Foreign Affairs in Beijing, both parties had a return agreement. The agreement at the time stipulated that the returned Italian Boxer Indemnity would be used to manage educational and charitable causes between China and Italy, and designated that a certain amount of the funds be used to open the port of Haizhou, dredge the Huai River, and build the Cao'e River Bridge. Therefore, the issue of the Italian Boxer Indemnity not only being suspended for one year is not a problem, but the issue of continued returns can also be discussed. The date on which the new Italian envoy, Ciano, will present his credentials in Beijing cannot be determined at this time because the credentials have not yet arrived in Shanghai.

Telegraph Workers Staged a Half-Day Strike Yesterday Afternoon 130

Fully Resumed Work After Persuasion in the Evening Each Person Will Receive an Additional Two Yuan Implemented in Stages

International Telegraph Company, Radio Telegraph General Bureau, Telegraph Bureau All workers, due to demands to improve treatment and universally increase wages by three yuan, were unsuccessful. Yesterday afternoon, they carried out a strike. Afterwards, after talks between the Director of the Telegraph Administration, Zhong E, and worker representatives, work fully resumed at 7:00 PM. The detailed circumstances are as follows:

Unsuccessful Demands The telegraph workers at the Lao Bei Men Radio Telegraph General Bureau, the Sima Road China Telegraph Bureau, and the Renji Road Sassoon Building International Telegraph Company, demanded improved treatment and a universal increase in wages of three yuan per month. This was approved by the Ministry of Communications, divided into four grades of increase: (A) an increase of 5 jiao, (B) an increase of 1 yuan, (C) an increase of 1.5 yuan, and (D) an increase of 2 yuan, with increases determined by work performance. All workers expressed dissatisfaction and insisted on a minimum universal wage increase of two yuan per month.

Staged a Strike The China Telegraph Bureau on Sima Road, which sends and receives domestic and international wired telegraphs, employs a total of 65 telegraph delivery workers. Due to repeated requests to improve treatment, which had not been granted, they collectively staged a strike on the morning of the previous day at 11:00 AM to awaken the authorities. As a result, telegrams arriving at the station lacked delivery personnel and had to be temporarily suspended. Afterwards, Bureau Chief Rong Baofeng invited worker representatives and persuaded the workers to resume work first, stating that he fully accepted the workers' request to increase wages by two yuan and would immediately report it to the Ministry of Communications for approval. Consequently, all workers resumed work at 2:00 PM.

Sending Telegrams as Usual The Lao Bei Men Radio Telegraph General Bureau, which specializes in sending and receiving domestic wireless telegrams, employs 48 workers. The International Telegraph Company on Renji Road, which specializes in sending and receiving foreign wireless telegrams, employs 32 workers. All workers, because the authorities still had not agreed to the wage increase and the wages they received were insufficient to live on, had no choice but to jointly stage a strike at 2:30 PM yesterday afternoon. As a result, telegrams arriving in Shanghai at these two telegraph companies lacked delivery personnel and were temporarily suspended. However, sending telegrams continued as usual, and by 6:00 PM, there were over 300 items piled up.

Workers Petition The International Telegraph Company workers sent representatives Yang Ziqing and Qian Haiping. The Radio Telegraph Company workers sent representatives Liu Youliang, Gu Yuesheng, and Zhu Xunlin. They all went to the International Telegraph Bureau on Jing'an Temple Road and Mu'er Ming Road to petition, and the Telegraph Bureau workers also sent Ding Wenhe, Yang Zhicheng, and Jiang Hongdu to show their support. As for the striking workers, they all followed the petitioning representatives and gathered in the garden of the International Telegraph Bureau.

Workers' Statement Yesterday, a worker representative gave a statement to the New Voice News Agency, saying, "When the Radio Telegraph Company was under the management of the Construction Committee, wages were increased twice a year, in January and June, by two yuan each time. Since the Ministry of Communications took over, wages have been increased only once a year. The usual minimum wage is 15 yuan, and the maximum is 25 yuan, with food and lodging provided by the workers themselves. There was no increase last year, and as of July 1st of this year, there was still no increase, so we contacted the Radio Telegraph Company workers to request an increase. This is really a matter of last resort, and we hope that all sectors will understand."

Persuaded to Return to Work The Director of the Telegraph Administration and Acting Director of the International Telegraph Bureau, Zhong E, ordered the worker representatives to explain to the workers that a strike by communications industry workers is of great importance to public security and persuaded them to resume work first. He fully accepted the request for a two-yuan wage increase. However, the Shanghai General Bureau would implement the increase starting in August of this year, and the International Telegraph Company would implement the increase starting in January of next year. The worker representatives then withdrew and reported the accepted persuasion to the workers, and at 7:00 PM they announced the resumption of work.

Northeast Postal Service Changes Blockade Measures 131

South Manchurian Railway Area Postal services to the Northeast will be delivered as usual from yesterday. After the Ministry of Communications ordered the Postal Administration to implement a blockade, the South Manchurian Railway area was also included in the blockade. Later, after the Postal Director Lin Shi arrived in Shanghai and consulted with Postal Director-General Huang Naishu several times, they slightly changed the previously determined blockade measures and decided to open postal services to the South Manchurian Railway area and receive and send mail as usual. The delivery route was changed to delivery via Dalian. Yesterday morning (the 2nd), Postal Director-General Huang Naishu issued a special order to the Shanghai Administration to comply with the regulations. The Administration Director Zha Peilin immediately informed the staff, so that all would be aware. Therefore, starting yesterday afternoon, the bureau has accepted and sent mail to the South Manchurian Railway area, but the blockade will remain in effect outside the railway area. Furthermore, the Shanghai Postal Administration also issued order No. 1607, informing postal staff to accept airmail lightweight mail to Europe. The original order stated, "In order to inform you, all bureaus may accept mail from Saigon to Marseilles. They should all handle it in accordance with the provisions opened in [Postal Bureau No. 776]."

Northeast Postal Workers Arrive at Customs Successively to Report 133

Difficult to Escape from Jilin-Heilongjiang Region Due to Surveillance Negotiations with Barlidi Have Not Yet Yielded Results

Postal Director Lin Shi had not yet returned to Beijing yesterday. In the morning, he went to the Postal Administration to discuss official business with Huang Naishu. The official report regarding the investigation of the establishment of post offices by the Japanese had not yet arrived at the bureau. However, the postal staff of the three northeastern provinces are now a key issue following the blockade of the Northeast postal service. According to reports received by the Postal Administration, as of yesterday, a total of nine people had returned from outside the customs area and reported to Shanghai: four people served in the Jilin-Heilongjiang region, and five people served in the Shenyang region. A total of 98 people reported to Tianjin: 27 postal officers, 15 postal assistants, and 56 messengers and workers. Many people have also successively reported to Shandong Province, but the exact number is unknown. As for the postal staff currently in the three regions of Jilin, Heilongjiang, and Shenyang, the total number is over 2,000. The situation now is that the issue of the staff in the Shenyang region returning is easier than in the Jilin-Heilongjiang region. This is because the Shenyang region was prepared when the puppet state took over, so there was no shortage of people working. However, in the Jilin-Heilongjiang region, the postal workers were instigated by the puppet state's postal director, and the puppet government issued an order to all landlords stating that if postal personnel lived in their homes and were allowed to escape, only the landlords would be questioned. Therefore, the issue of returning has become more difficult. Northeast Postal Director Barlidi has been strongly negotiating with the puppet state, but it is unknown when there will be results.

Interview with Postal Workers from the Jilin-Heilongjiang Region Arriving in Shanghai 134

Jilin City Post Office Losses Exceed 130,000 Yuan, Emuyang Postmaster Killed by Japanese Troops, Anti-Japanese Volunteers Appear Everywhere, Japanese Feeling Helpless, According to Guo Wen Agency: Yesterday, the reporter met with two postal workers, Zhu and Chen (names requested not to be published), from the Jilin-Heilongjiang region who had arrived in Shanghai at their residence. They were asked about the postal service and political situation in the Northeast. Their accounts were filled with immeasurable sorrow and indignation. We, the people living peacefully within the Great Wall, living like swallows in a safe nest or fish in a pot, seemingly unaware that the map of the Northeast has changed color, should sigh with regret. The following is a record of their accounts, which can be summarized as follows: The two of us worked at the Jilin City Post Office. The postal districts of the three northeastern provinces are divided into two regions: Liaoning and Jilin-Heilongjiang. The Liaoning region's general office is in Shenyang, and the postal director is Barritt. The Jilin-Heilongjiang region is formed by the merger of Jilin and Heilongjiang provinces, and the general office is located in Harbin, with Smith as the postal director. The total number of personnel in both regions, including postal workers and laborers, is between 2,800 and 2,900, with the Jilin-Heilongjiang region accounting for 1,500 to 1,600. We received orders on the 25th of last month and took a train to Dalian the next day. Because our ancestral homes are in Zhejiang and Guangdong, we came directly from Dalian to Shanghai and arrived at the port on the 31st. The postal and local political situation in the Jilin-Heilongjiang region is extremely chaotic. Initially, the puppet state's postal director, the Japanese Fujiwara, publicly stated that the postal service of the three provinces would be taken over on August 1st. In reality, this was a strategy to appease the postal workers. Suddenly, on the 24th and 25th, they forcibly seized control. Therefore, we learned of the news on the 25th and also received the official order to enter the customs, so we stopped going to the office. If we had gone, we would have been detained or placed under surveillance. The various coercive and oppressive measures were worse than those in a colony. Currently, the Jilin first-class postmaster, Chen Weiping, and the Changchun postmaster, Li Kede, are both under Japanese surveillance. Among the twelve people wanted by the puppet state, seven or eight have been arrested. Li Rulin, the former director of the parcel tax office, has been temporarily appointed by the puppet state as the Jilin postmaster, and Jin Zhenmin, the son-in-law of the puppet state's Minister of Communications, has been appointed as the Changchun postmaster. All postal affairs of the puppet state are handled under the direction of the Japanese Fujiwara. The losses, in terms of real estate alone, for the Jilin Province Post Office exceed 130,000 yuan, not including other losses such as remittances, stamps, and a small number of cash remittances. When we departed from Jilin, the administration of the three provinces could be said to have been almost completely destroyed. Recently, the postal service was managed to a conclusion by the two postal directors, Barritt and Smith. The puppet state, recognizing the lack of specialized personnel, is willing to use a large amount of money to bribe lower-level postal workers to stay. In some places, because everyone has fled, it is impossible to deliver mail. Therefore, they have no choice but to use postal workers who are more familiar with the area. Thus, there are even cases where postal workers have become postmasters in several post offices. The extremity of their predicament can be imagined. Local resistance to the Japanese is becoming increasingly enthusiastic. Anti-Japanese volunteers in groups of fifty or one hundred appear everywhere. When they encounter a small number of enemies, they surround and annihilate them. When a large force comes to reinforce them, they retreat. As a result, they are constantly on the move. The anti-Japanese volunteers are not only familiar with the terrain but also have complete weapons. Therefore, the Japanese also feel helpless in the face of this. The most powerful anti-Japanese volunteer force in Jilin Province is Wang Delin's, which has been joined by patriotic individuals one after another and now exceeds 300,000. It must be said that it is a powerful force. The Japanese are brutal beyond human comprehension. They use all kinds of methods of killing, including beheading and dismemberment. For example, a resident of Liaoning Province sent a letter from Nanjing, and if the words contained any dissatisfaction with the puppet state, he would be arrested by the Japanese army and is still in prison to this day. Even within the postal service in Jilin Province, there was a postmaster named Yang (his given name is unknown) at the Emuyang Post Office. When the Japanese army sent a team to forcibly take over the office, Yang was drafting a telegram to report the puppet state's forced seizure of the postal service in the Northeast. The Japanese obtained a copy of the telegram and immediately took him away. His fate is unknown to this day. According to rumors, Yang is no longer alive and was shot by the Japanese army. Furthermore, if passersby discuss politics and are interrogated by Japanese agents, they are forcibly identified as anti-Japanese volunteers and subjected to whipping and other tortures without end. Speaking of this causes deep pain. We are very fortunate to have escaped the tiger's den. He went on to say that he had already reported to the general office and was currently preparing a report. The general office had agreed to find a way to arrange their lives, but the specific location had not yet been determined.

Various Industries Continue to Resist Foreign Goods 135

Since the appearance of the Blood Soul Assassination Squad, the sale of inferior goods has stopped immediately, proving to be very effective. All industries have also reorganized their inspection efforts. The following is a record of the news obtained yesterday:

Statement from the Nanjing Road Business Association: This port received a letter yesterday from the Nanjing Road Business Association stating, "We, the members of this association, have always been at the forefront of patriotic advocacy and practical action to save the country. Our actions are clear and have long been recognized by society. Furthermore, we are honored to be the most prosperous business group on Nanjing Road in Shanghai. Knowing that the actions of our members will be closely watched by all sectors at home and abroad, we are making every effort to promote domestic products and resist foreign goods, striving to set an example. Since the September 18th Incident, at the request of a majority of our members, we have strictly sealed off foreign goods and repeatedly sent inspectors to ensure that all stores have cleared and stopped selling them. After the end of the Shanghai War, a small number of stores, constrained by economic stagnation, cleaned up and sold off their old inventory, or have already sold their businesses and mixed in foreign goods. Our association is deeply concerned that a small number of unscrupulous elements, beyond the reach of our authority and unable to be controlled, will damage the reputation of all stores on the road and arouse criticism from all sectors in Shanghai. Therefore, on the one hand, we are advising all members and non-member stores to correct their behavior if they have done wrong and to make greater efforts if they have not. On the other hand, we are repeatedly convening meetings to discuss appropriate measures to ensure that all stores on this road can act in good conscience, voluntarily commit to never buying or selling foreign goods. Unexpectedly, a group called the Blood Soul Assassination Squad has recently used extraordinary means to stop unscrupulous merchants. Yesterday, they sent a letter to our association, ordering us to advise our members to clear out foreign goods within a time limit. Their righteousness and fervor are evident on paper and are understood by society. It is our association's duty to work harder. However, the actions of this group are prone to legal pitfalls, which may please our enemies or even cause unexpected disturbances. It seems that they should be cautious in their actions. Since the letter has no address, our association cannot answer in detail. We respectfully use the newspapers to express our sincere advice and solemnly declare to our patriotic compatriots, hoping that they will observe carefully. Shanghai Nanjing Road Business Association."

Letter from the Match Industry Association: The All-China Match Industry Association, fearing that its member factories would become lax in resisting Japanese goods over time, sent a special letter to its member factories yesterday stating, "Dear Sirs, Since the Wanxian Incident and the September 18th Incident last year, the Chinese people have been indignant at the barbarity of Japanese imperialism and have continued to resist foreign goods. For a time, Japanese goods disappeared from the market. However, after the signing of the Shanghai War Armistice Agreement, Japanese goods reappeared and have recently regained their position as the number one imported goods. In this situation, not only has the goal of resisting foreign goods not been achieved, but also all previous efforts have been wasted. We are deeply saddened by this. Therefore, we are sending this special letter to advise all our members to adhere to their original intentions, persevere to the end, reject all Japanese materials, and never willingly join the ranks of unscrupulous merchants. This is of utmost importance."

Yongan Foreign Goods Still Sealed: The Yongan Company on Nanjing Road also received a warning from the Blood Soul Squad. A reporter from the New Voice Society visited Mr. Guo, the general manager of the company, yesterday to inquire about the company's response to the Assassination Squad's warning. Mr. Guo replied, "Since the Northeast Incident, all foreign goods have been sealed and sales have been stopped. At that time, the Anti-Japanese Association clearly identified the number of items, separately recorded them, and sealed them. They remain sealed and can be inspected at any time." The reporter then asked, "Since your company's old foreign goods have been sealed, are you now indirectly importing foreign goods privately?" Mr. Guo said, "This is even more unreasonable. The old foreign goods are still sealed. Why would we spend more money to buy new ones? Even the most foolish person would not do this. Furthermore, one hand cannot cover the eyes and ears of the world. All sectors can conduct close inspections at any time, and the truth will be revealed."

Clothing Industry Association Implements Inspections: Since the September 18th Incident, the Clothing Industry Association immediately established an inspection team to conduct mutual inspections on the transportation of clothing packages, with excellent results. Later, the Anti-Japanese Association was ordered to stop, and the association's inspection team also stopped at the same time. Yesterday's newspaper reported that several transport companies were found to be mixing and smuggling inferior goods in clothing packages, which caused great indignation. Therefore, they have reorganized the inspection team and will immediately supervise each other and implement inspections.

Silk and Cotton Weaving Industry Held a General Meeting Yesterday: The silk and cotton weaving industry held a temporary membership meeting yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM to discuss thorough measures. More than 70 people attended, including Zhu Wenqi, Pan Xusheng, Qian Chenrong, Zhu Zhenhan, Guan Pingqin, Cui Fuzhuang, and Cao Youguang. First, Chairman Zhu Wenqi reported on the urgency of the national crisis and the measures for merchants to save themselves. Then, the discussion began. Under the enthusiastic atmosphere of the members, they unanimously voted to actively use domestic goods and thoroughly eliminate inferior goods. The measures were divided into (A) notifying all members to actively report, (B) contacting relevant industries to conduct a unified investigation, etc. Pan Xusheng was appointed to contact the Cotton Cloth Industry Association first. (C) Dyeing factories, cloth factories, and cloth shops were divided into groups to study and discuss detailed plans and submit them to the Executive Committee for handling. Guan Pingqin, Yin Shuqiao, Gu Yongquan, Zhang Minglun, Zhu Gengtao, Zhu Maoting, and Zheng Jirong were appointed as members of the Dyeing Factory Group, with Guan Pingqin as the convener. Zhu Zhenhan, Xu Yangnan, Guan Bingqing, Qian Chenrong, He Dehuai, Cao Youguang, and Yan Guangdi were appointed as members of the Cloth Factory Group, with Qian Chenrong as the convener. The Cloth Shop Group was to appoint its own members and report to the association. All groups were required to convene meetings within one week. The meeting adjourned after 6:00 PM.

Grain Association Investigates Japanese Rice: Ten companies, including Zaliang Youbing Tongye Nanshi Zhabei Dingfeng Hengxing and Heji, purchased a large quantity of Japanese rice. After the industry association reported this to the Grain Association, the association held a special meeting on the 27th of last month and summoned the companies to the meeting to question them. They all said that the foreign rice they purchased was purchased from Tongxingtai and was brokered by brokers. They did not order it from Japanese foreign firms. If they did not believe it, they could check the accounts. The association sent personnel to conduct a thorough investigation and sent a letter to Tongxingtai asking when the rice was shipped, on what ship it was transported, how much there was, and whether it was registered, requesting a prompt reply. The association received a reply yesterday and immediately convened a meeting of the industry association in the afternoon, chaired by Cai Yukun, to report on the progress of the situation and read the letter from Tongxingtai to the association. They asked the industry association to discuss the measures. After discussion, the industry association believed that Tongxingtai was entrusted by a certain Japanese foreign firm to sell the rice and that the industry association was unaware of this and was deceived into purchasing it. Now that the companies reported that they purchased it from Tongxingtai, and Tongxingtai's reply was slightly inconsistent, the matter should be investigated. After deliberation, the association instructed Tongxingtai to store the arrived goods in which warehouse and send a sample sheet to the association. After arriving at the warehouse, samples of the rice would be taken and another meeting would be held for public inspection to discuss the measures.

Hurricane Changes Direction 136

Will Not Come to Shanghai

The Zi Lin newspaper reports that the hurricane was heading north from near Taiwan, and for a time, it seemed likely to head straight for Shanghai. However, yesterday (the 1st), the Xujiahui Observatory received a report that it had changed direction to the northeast and was blowing towards the Yellow Sea, causing a strong easterly wind in the Yangtze River basin. It is said that the hurricane was no more than 60 miles from Shanghai at its closest point.

Incense Industry Workers' Union Decides to Resume Work Today 137

Labor-Management Conditions Awaiting Mediation

After the incense industry workers went on strike to demand improved treatment, the Party and government authorities advised them to resume work first. Yesterday, the Workers' Union decided to fully resume work starting today, and labor-management conditions will be mediated according to the law. The details are as follows:

Union Meeting: The Incense Industry Occupational Union went to the Party and government authorities the day before yesterday to request mediation. Yesterday, the Social Affairs Bureau advised them to resume work first. Therefore, a joint meeting of the directors and supervisors was held yesterday morning at 10:00 AM at the union's office at No. 91 Dajili. Li Weixiong from the Municipal Party Committee and Zhu Sen from the Social Affairs Bureau attended to advise them. All members were present, and the meeting was chaired by Yang Pansheng and recorded by Zhou Weixin. First, the chairman reported on the strike. Then, representatives from the Party and government authorities gave advice. It was decided on the spot that (1) in order to respect the advice of the Party and government authorities, all workers would resume work starting tomorrow (the 3rd). (2) The Party and government authorities were requested to convene a mediation between the two parties within three days. (3) The wage increase of 40% was still requested. (4) Diao Jinlin and Zhu Liansheng, were condemned as capitalists' lackeys who colluded with hooligans to force workers in Pudong to resume work. In addition to being expelled from the union, the Party and government authorities were requested to severely punish them.

Notice of Resumption of Work: The Incense Industry Occupational Union issued a notice to all workers last night stating, "Notice: After investigating, all workers in this industry were unable to withstand the oppression of the capitalists and were forced to go on strike automatically on the afternoon of July 28th. However, they were able to maintain order, which is commendable. Now, in accordance with the advice of the Party and government authorities, it is proposed to resume work on the 3rd. However, because our group is far away and transportation is inconvenient, work will be delayed until the 4th. Representatives of the Party and government authorities have verbally promised to convene a mediation within three days. If the capitalists continue to be cunning, we will submit a request to the higher authorities for review. Please be informed. This is to notify you."

Mediation to be Held Soon: Starting at 7:00 PM yesterday, incense workers in the Hakka group began preparing incense materials in the workshops in accordance with the union's orders and were scheduled to officially resume work today. However, most of the workers in this group are in Gaoqiao and other places. Due to the limited time, they will need to enter the workshops this afternoon to prepare incense materials and officially resume work tomorrow morning. In addition, the Social Affairs Bureau, because the workers accepted the advice of the Party and government authorities, decided to formally convene a labor-management mediation within the next few days.

Establishment of the Money Industry Joint Reserve 138

Grand Opening Meeting Held Yesterday

Fifteen Executive Committee Members Elected

The Shanghai Money Industry Association held its tenth membership representative meeting yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM at the association's office on Ningbo Road to formally establish the Money Industry Joint Reserve. The charter was approved, and a resolution was passed to issue a declaration on the abolition of taels and the adoption of the yuan. The following is a record of the meeting:

Attending Representatives: Approximately 80 companies, including Dade, Dalai, Yuanda, Yuansheng, Wu, Renheng, Yongju, Yong, Yongfeng, Ankang, Anyu, Cunde, Tongan, Tongchun, Tongtai, Xin, Yu, Zhiyu, Zhicheng, Junchang, Jintai, Changsheng, Chengyu, Da, Yifeng, Xinfu, Xinkang, Xinyu, Hengxiang, Hengxun, Henglong, Henglai, Chunyuan, Hengfeng, Houchun, Yida, Yichang, Yikang, Yishen, Yifeng, Zhixiang, Zhentai, Qianyuan, Yintai, Shunkang, Dunyu, Huifeng, Yisheng, Yichang, Yixing, Ruichang, Yuansheng, Futai, Fukang, Fuyuan, Shenyi, Huichang, Gengyu, Jukang, Rongkang, Dechang, Zikang, Zifeng, Qingda, Qingcheng, Ruikang, Dingsheng, Zhengxiang, Hengjiu, Hengtong, Hongxiang, Hongsheng, Hongfeng, Baochang, Baofeng, Baoda, and Shengchang, and more than 120 representatives, including Qin Runqing, Yu Zuoting, Pei Yunqing, and Hu Xisheng.

Meeting Details: After Chairman Qin Runqing performed the ceremonial rites, he reported on (1) the minutes of the previous meeting, (2) the documents received and sent in the past month, and (3) the number of times industry representatives gathered at the association in July. Then, the charter and declaration were approved, and a total of four cases were discussed. Next, fifteen executive committee members were elected. The meeting adjourned at 4:00 PM.

Resolutions Passed: The following important cases were resolved: (1) Please make a public decision on the July discount interest. Resolution: 3.95 discount. (2) The Special Property Custody Committee of the Industry Association was resolved by the management meeting on July 18th to be reorganized into the Shanghai Money Industry Joint Reserve. Please retroactively approve the case. Resolution: Approved. (3) The management meeting on July 18th resolved that each member of the industry association should increase its cash fund by 15,000 silver yuan in order to strengthen its financial resources. The resolution has already been implemented. Please retroactively approve the case. Resolution: Approved. (4) Please decide on the draft charter of the Industry Association Joint Reserve. Resolution: Amended and approved. (5) Elect fifteen executive committee members and three inspection committee members of the reserve. Resolution: The executive committee members will be filled by the first session of the association's committee members, and the inspection committee members will be elected by vote at a later date. (6) Regarding business matters of the industry association and the abolition of taels and the adoption of the yuan, it was resolved to issue a declaration and hand it over to the secretary-general to draft.

List of Committee Members: List of executive committee members of the Joint Reserve: Qin Runqing, Pei Yunqing, Hu Xisheng, Xie Fupu, Li Shoushan, Lou Xunru, Wang Bokan, Sheng Xiaoshan, Zhao Shushan, Chuan Songnian, Li Jisheng, Wang Juru, Yu Zuoting, Wang Huailian, and Xu Boxi. The five standing committee members are Qin Runqing, Hu Xisheng, Yu Zuoting, Pei Yunqing, and Fu Songnian. Qin Runqing is the chairman.

Original Charter Text: The original charter text approved by the general meeting is as follows: Shanghai Money Industry Joint Reserve Charter, Chapter 1, General Provisions, Article 1: The Shanghai Money Industry Association, for the sake of all members, to consolidate the foundation, regulate finance, and specially establish a public treasury to handle joint reserve matters, is named the Shanghai Money Industry Joint Reserve. Article 2: This Joint Reserve is jointly established by the industry. All members of this association may be basic members of this reserve. Yuanci counterparts who wish to join may also be called members. Article 3: This reserve is a permanent institution. Basic members and members may not withdraw halfway unless they cease business. Article 4: This reserve may not engage in external business. Article 5: This reserve shall use local newspapers for public announcements and official letters for internal notifications. Chapter 2, Reserve Assets and Cash, Article 6: The amount of reserve assets and cash of this reserve shall be as follows and shall be paid by the fund members: (1) Assets of 27 million yuan, basic members must deposit at least 300,000 yuan or more in estimated value of silver yuan, and members shall pay half of that amount, with no restrictions on larger amounts. (2) Cash of 3 million yuan shall be paid by basic members and members, and the amount to be paid shall be determined separately. Article 7: This reserve shall accept the following types of reserve assets only: (A) Goods warehouse receipts that can be immediately converted into cash; (B) Real estate with an estimated value in this city; (C) Cash coins or cash notes; (D) Baoda notes or silver yuan. Article 8: If the price of reserve assets rises or falls, this reserve may notify the increase or decrease at any time. Article 9: Reserve assets may be exchanged by the depositor for assets of equivalent estimated value at any time, but may not be less than the provisions of Article 6, paragraph 1. Chapter 3, Custody Receipts, Article 10: This reserve shall issue custody receipts immediately upon receiving reserve assets and cash. Chapter 4, Tasks, Article 11: The tasks of this reserve are as follows: (1) Handling the matters of silver and silver yuan receipts and settlements for the industry with banks; (2) Handling the deposit and payment of funds for the industry; (3) Handling the discounting of bills for the industry; (4) Handling the exchange and transfer of notes for the industry; (5) Handling the receipt and exchange of notes for the industry association; (6) Handling the necessary facilities for the industry. Article 12: Basic members and members may open current accounts in this reserve for the purpose of registering receipts and payments on the following two tasks: (1) Bank receipts and settlements, deposits shall be made if there is a surplus, and overdrafts shall be made if there is a deficiency, the amount of the overdraft and the interest rate shall be determined separately; (2) Note exchange, shall be handled in accordance with the above provision. Chapter 5, Organization, Article 13: The Basic Member Representative Assembly shall be the highest authority of this reserve. Article 14: This reserve shall have fifteen executive committee members, who shall be concurrently held by the current members of this association. When the members of this association are re-elected and replaced, the members of this reserve shall be replaced at the same time. Article 15: This reserve shall have five standing committee members, who shall be concurrently held by the current standing committee members of this association. Article 16: This reserve shall have one chairman, who shall be concurrently held by the current chairman of this association. Article 17: This reserve shall have three inspection committee members, who shall be elected by the Basic Member Representative Assembly, with a term of one year and may be re-elected. Article 18: This reserve shall have one manager, who shall be appointed by the Executive Committee. The manager shall consult with the chairman and standing committee members to handle all daily tasks. Article 19: The business of this reserve shall be divided into three sections: accounting, cashier, and documentation. Each section shall have one director and a number of clerks, all of whom shall be appointed by the manager in consultation with the chairman and standing committee members. Chapter 6, Executive Committee, Article 20: The powers of the Executive Committee are as follows: (1) Matters concerning the collection, valuation, custody, and disposal of reserve assets and cash; (2) Matters concerning the design of basic members and members; (3) Matters concerning the review and approval of various rules of this reserve; (4) Matters concerning the preparation of budgets; (5) Supervising all tasks of this reserve; (6) Inspecting all account books and vouchers of this reserve; (7) Taking inventory of reserve assets and cash; (8) Reviewing and approving budgets and final accounts. Article 21: The Executive Committee shall hold at least one regular meeting per month. Temporary meetings may be convened by the chairman at any time. Article 22: Resolutions of the Executive Committee shall be passed with the attendance of more than two-thirds of the executive committee members and with the consent of a majority of those present. Article 23: If an executive committee member is unable to attend due to circumstances, he may entrust another executive committee member to act as his proxy. Article 24: The minutes of the Executive Committee meeting shall be recorded, signed by the chairman, and preserved. Chapter 7, Basic Member Representative Assembly, Article 25: The Basic Member Representative Assembly shall hold a regular meeting twice a year, on January 2nd and July 2nd, convened by the Executive Committee. If the Executive Committee deems it necessary, or if more than one-third of the basic members request a meeting in writing, a temporary meeting may be convened at any time. Article 26: The opening of the Basic Member Representative Assembly requires the attendance of more than two-thirds of the representatives of the basic members. Article 27: Resolutions of the Basic Member Representative Assembly shall be passed with the consent of more than two-thirds of the representatives present. Article 29: The resolutions of the Basic Member Representative Assembly shall be recorded, signed by the chairman, and preserved. Chapter 8, Accounting, Article 30: This reserve shall handle the final accounts once every six months, at the end of June and the end of December, and prepare the following reports: (1) Balance sheet; (2) Profit and loss statement; (3) Property catalog; (4) Report on reserve assets and cash; (5) Statistics on the tasks of this reserve. Chapter 9, Inspection, Article 31: After each final account, the inspection committee members shall verify all accounts, assets, and cash. Chapter 10, Supplementary Provisions, Article 32: The detailed rules for the operation of this reserve shall be formulated separately. Article 33: This charter shall be implemented after being resolved by the Basic Member Representative Assembly, and the same shall apply to amendments. Article 34: If there are any matters not covered by this charter, the Executive Committee may amend them at any time and submit them to the Basic Representative Assembly for approval and implementation.
